SVC Object Navigator - Partial T4

  • shortcuts
    • Quorum scan commands for manual T3
  • tasks
    • Show Original File
    • Apply a stored Fabric
    • Pull in Fabric from DumpDecoder
    • Browse objects in the snap
    • Apply a manual query
    • Apply a saved query
    • Delete this snap
  • reports
    • Health Test Report
    • Table of Objects
    • IO Group Memory Usage
    • SAN Connectivity
    • Cluster Audit Report

This page lists several svctask commands that can be used during manual T3 or T4 (or hybrid) recoveries in which the config file cannot be used directly. Use cases:

  • Performing a manual T3 recovery using a config file from an older code level than cannot be used by svcconfig recover
  • Recreating VDisks/Host maps after having to delete a pool due to data loss
Limitations:
  • Does not support VDisks with multiple copies
  • Does not support image mode VDisks
  • Does not add addditional access IO groups

All VDisks that could not be processed will be lised separately below

The following commands are available:
  • Enable Autoexpand for all space-efficient and compressed VDisks
  • Set the sync rate to default for all VDisks
  • svctask mkhost commands to create all FC hosts
  • chvdisk -name commands to rename all VDisks
  • mkvdisk commands to create all VDisks for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR-10KRPM (0)
  • mkvdiskhostmap commands to create all host mappings for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR-10KRPM (0)
  • mkvdisk commands to create all VDisks for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR2-10KRPM (1)
  • mkvdiskhostmap commands to create all host mappings for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR2-10KRPM (1)
  • mkvdisk commands to create all VDisks for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR-15KRPM (2)
  • mkvdiskhostmap commands to create all host mappings for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR-15KRPM (2)
  • mkvdisk commands to create all VDisks for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR-PERFORM-15KRPM (3)
  • mkvdiskhostmap commands to create all host mappings for MDisk Group IOGRP0-DR-PERFORM-15KRPM (3)
  • mkvdisk commands to create all VDisks for MDisk Group IOGRP01_DR_10K-900GB VMWARE (4)
  • mkvdiskhostmap commands to create all host mappings for MDisk Group IOGRP01_DR_10K-900GB VMWARE (4)
  • mkvdisk commands to create all VDisks for MDisk Group IOGRP01_DR_15K-300G (5)
  • mkvdiskhostmap commands to create all host mappings for MDisk Group IOGRP01_DR_15K-300G (5)

Enable Autoexpand for all space-efficient and compressed VDisks


  • svcinfo lssevdiskcopy -gui -nohdr | while read id name cid rest; do svctask chvdisk -autoexpand on -copy $cid $id; done

Set the sync rate to default for all VDisks


  • svcinfo lsvdisk -gui -nohdr | while read id rest; do svctask chvdisk -syncrate 50 $id; done

mkhost commands for all Fibre Channel Hosts


Does not support iSCSI/SAS/... hosts
